[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the Wireshark JSON [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`packet-json.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during fuzzing operations. The issue manifests as a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read operation beyond the bounds of a [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m-byte heap-allocated buffer, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurring in the `json_string_unescape` function at line [0m[1;36m361[0m[39m. This is triggered [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen processing JSON input containing Unicode surrogate escape sequences.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability, specifically a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read operation [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccessing memory immediately after an allocated buffer. AddressSanitizer has [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39massigned it a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m, categorizing it as a [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"1-byte-read-heap-buffer-overflow."[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability occurs during the parsing of a JSON string containing Unicode [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mescape sequences. The specific test input that triggers the issue is:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m[39m\n  [0m[32m"surrogates"[0m[39m: [0m[32m"\\U0000d83d\\U0000"[0m[39m\n[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m\n\n[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe memory violation happens at address `[0m[1;36m0x50300012dcd3[0m[39m`, which is located exactly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after a [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m-byte allocated region [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x50300012dcc0[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x50300012dcd3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicates an off-by-one error where the code attempts to read one byte past the end[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the allocated buffer.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Call Stack Analysis[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe error propagates through the following call sequence:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **`json_string_unescape`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-json.[0m[1;92mc:361[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - The point where the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds read occurs[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **`get_json_string`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-json.[0m[1;92mc:567[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Calls the unescape function[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **`after_value`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-json.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Processing after parsing a JSON value[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **`execute_callbacks`** and **`tvbparse_get`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvbparse.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - TVB parsing [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minfrastructure[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **`dissect_json`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-json.[0m[1;92mc:797[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - Main JSON dissection entry point[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Packet dissection infrastructure** - Standard Wireshark dissection chain[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Memory Allocation Context[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe problematic buffer was allocated through the following sequence:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `realloc` called from `g_realloc`[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `wmem_strbuf_finalize` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwmem_strbuf.[0m[1;92mc:388[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - String buffer finalization[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `get_json_string` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-json.[0m[1;92mc:564[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - JSON string extraction[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis suggests the buffer is used to construct a string during JSON parsing, and the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfinalization process determines the final buffer size before the unescape operation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis performed.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Analysis of the Issue[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe evaluation report identifies a **heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability** in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`epan/dissectors/packet-json.c` at line [0m[1;36m361[0m[39m within the `json_string_unescape` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction. The vulnerability occurs when processing Unicode surrogate pairs using [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe `\U` escape sequence format [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[39m hex digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Cause:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe code at lines [0m[1;36m359[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m368[0m[39m handles the case where a lead surrogate from `\U` is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowed by another `\U` escape sequence for the trail surrogate. This loop [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts to read [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m hex digits but **lacks critical safety checks** that are present[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min all other similar loops throughout the function:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Missing bounds check** before line [0m[1;36m361[0m[39m: No verification that `read_index < [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring_length` before accessing `string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mread_index[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Missing nibble validation** after line [0m[1;36m364[0m[39m: No check that `[0m[1;35mws_xton[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returned[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma valid hex digit [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>= [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather than [0m[1;36m-1[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No error recovery**: The loop doesn't set `is_valid_unicode_character = false`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand break on errors[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Trigger Condition:**[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe test case `\U0000d83d\U0000` exposes this bug:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `\U0000d83d` is parsed as a valid lead surrogate [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0xd83d[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The code detects it needs a trail surrogate and finds `\U`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The loop expects [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m hex digits but only [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m exist [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;36m0000[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before the closing quote[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When `[0m[33mi[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`, `read_index` points beyond the [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m-byte buffer boundary, causing a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read overflow[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Comprehensive Fix Implementation[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix must be applied to **epan/dissectors/packet-json.c** at lines [0m[1;36m359[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m368[0m[39m. The [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrected loop should follow the exact pattern used consistently in [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m other [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocations within the same function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m269[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m291[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m319[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m341[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m422[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m444[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m472[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m494[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Patch Location:** `epan/dissectors/packet-json.[0m[1;92mc:359[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m368[0m[39m`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Required Changes:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe loop at lines [0m[1;36m359[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m368[0m[39m must be modified to include:[0m                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Add nibble validation AFTER line [0m[1;36m364[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter ws_xton call[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnibble < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The bitwise operations at lines [0m[1;36m366[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m367[0m[39m should only execute after validation [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpasses[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This is the Optimal Approach:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Consistency with Existing Code**: This exact pattern appears [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m times in the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msame function at lines [0m[1;36m269[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m291[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39minitial `\U`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m319[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m341[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\u` after `\U` lead[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m422[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m444[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39minitial `\u`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and [0m[1;36m472[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m494[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\u` after `\u` lead[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The fix simply applies [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe established pattern to the one location where it was inadvertently omitted.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal Impact**: The fix only adds safety checks without altering the core [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic or functionality. The existing error handling mechanism [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`is_valid_unicode_character` flag[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is already in place and works correctly for all[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother cases.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `is_valid_unicode_character` flag is already checked at line [0m[1;36m396[0m[39m to decide[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhether to output the character or a replacement character[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The validation at lines [0m[1;36m370[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m already handles invalid trail surrogates[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m conversion at lines [0m[1;36m398[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m408[0m[39m remains unchanged[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Side Effects**: [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fix doesn't modify any function signatures[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to data structures or memory allocation[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The wmem_strbuf buffer management remains unchanged[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other escape sequence handlers continue to work identically[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Complete Error Handling**: When bounds are exceeded or invalid hex digits are [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mencountered:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The loop breaks immediately, preventing buffer overflow[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `is_valid_unicode_character` is set to false[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m412[0m[39m appends a Unicode replacement character [0m[1;39m([0m[39mU+FFFD[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Processing continues safely with the next character[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Addresses the Issues:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Prevents Heap-Buffer-Overflow**: The bounds check at line [0m[1;36m361[0m[39m ensures [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`read_index` never exceeds `string_length`, preventing out-of-bounds reads[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Handles Malformed Input**: Invalid hex digits [0m[1;39m([0m[39mresulting in `nibble < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetected and cause graceful failure[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintains Security**: No information leakage from reading beyond buffer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundaries[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserves Functionality**: Valid surrogate pairs continue to work correctly[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects and Mitigation:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Previously [0m[32m"Accepted"[0m[39m Malformed Input**: JSON strings with incomplete `\U` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mescape sequences that might have been processed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith undefined behavior due to the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now be handled by inserting a replacement character. This is the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect behavior per JSON specification.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Performance**: The two additional checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbounds and nibble validation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m add [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegligible overhead and match the pattern used throughout the function.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Backward Compatibility**: Since the previous behavior was undefined [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreading [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, there's no legitimate backward compatibility concern. The fix makes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior well-defined and secure.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Reference from Codebase:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix pattern is directly derived from the existing correct implementations in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same file:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m272[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m276[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m283[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m287[0m[39m: Pattern for `\U` initial parsing[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m326[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m333[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m337[0m[39m: Pattern for `\u` after `\U` lead surrogate[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m425[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m429[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m436[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m440[0m[39m: Pattern for `\u` initial parsing  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m475[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m479[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m486[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m490[0m[39m: Pattern for `\u` after `\u` lead surrogate[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll these sections demonstrate that the developer intended to use this safety [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern throughout, and the bug at lines [0m[1;36m359[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m368[0m[39m is simply an oversight that needs [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrection.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo implement this fix from the initial codebase:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Locate the vulnerable code** in `epan/dissectors/packet-json.c` at lines [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m359[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m368[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe loop within the `else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurrent_character == [0m[32m'U'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block that [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollows a lead surrogate detection from `\U`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Insert bounds check** immediately after the opening of the for loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m361[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add the check: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[39mread_index < string_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add the error handling: `is_valid_unicode_character = false; break;`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Include the comment: `[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Do not overflow input string`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Insert nibble validation** immediately after the `ws_xton` call [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m364[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add the check: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnibble < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add the error handling: `is_valid_unicode_character = false; break;`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Verify the fix** doesn't alter any other code paths:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The surrounding surrogate pair detection logic remains unchanged[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The error recovery mechanism at lines [0m[1;36m396[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m413[0m[39m remains unchanged[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No modifications to function parameters or return values[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Test with the provided test case**: The input `\U0000d83d\U0000` should now:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parse `\U0000d83d` successfully as a lead surrogate[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Detect it needs a trail surrogate[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Attempt to read [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m hex digits after `\U`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Break safely at iteration [0m[33mi[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m when bounds check fails[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Set `is_valid_unicode_character = false`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Append a replacement character instead of crashing[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix is surgical, consistent with the codebase, and resolves the security [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability without introducing any breaking changes.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
